GT: -c0*beta*v - omega0**c1*(gamma*Abs(v)**c2 + c3)*x - omega0**c4*x**c5 - omega0**c6*x
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed) simplifies to a concrete function of **x and v only** (no t-dependence):
\[
\text{GT}=-1.89974654282317\,v\;-\;3.43809390825923\,x^3\;-\;3.43809390825923\,x\,(0.0191974038845046|v|^{1/3}+1)\;-\;3.43809390825923\,x
\]
Combine the two linear-in-\(x\) terms:
\[
\text{GT}=-1.89974654282317\,v\;-\;3.43809390825923\,x^3\;-\;3.43809390825923\cdot 0.0191974038845046\,x|v|^{1/3}\;-\;6.87618781651846\,x
\]
So GT contains these essential structures:
- \(x^3\) term
- \(x\) term
- \(v\) term
- **cross term** \(x\,|v|^{1/3}\)
- **no** \(x^2,x^5,\dots\), **no** \(v|v|\), \(v^3\), etc.
- **no t dependence** (so any \(\cos(\cdot t)\), \(\exp(c t)\), etc. must be zeroed out by coefficients)

Now check candidates: to match GT, a candidate must be able (by choosing constants and possibly a domain restriction like \(v\ge 0\)) to reproduce **exactly** the \(x|v|^{1/3}\) dependence. None of the candidates include \(|v|^{1/3}\) or any fractional power of \(v\), nor any function of \(v\) multiplied by \(x\) except via polynomials like \(v x^2\), \(v x\cos(\cdot)\), \(v|v|\), \(v^3\), etc. A domain restriction cannot turn \(v\), \(v|v|\), \(v^3\), \(v x^2\), etc. into \(|v|^{1/3}\) for a continuous nontrivial domain. So this missing functional form is the key blocker.

## Ground Truth Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
`-1.89974654282317*v - 3.43809390825923*x**3 - 3.43809390825923*x*(0.0191974038845046*Abs(v)**0.333333333333333 + 1) - 3.43809390825923*x`

Let me simplify:
- Term 1: `-1.89974654282317*v`
- Term 2: `-3.43809390825923*x**3`
- Term 3: `-3.43809390825923*x*(0.0191974038845046*Abs(v)**(1/3) + 1)` = `-3.43809390825923*x - 3.43809390825923*0.0191974038845046*x*Abs(v)**(1/3)` = `-3.43809390825923*x - 0.0660046...*x*Abs(v)**(1/3)`
- Term 4: `-3.43809390825923*x`

Combining all terms:
- `v` term: `-1.89975*v`
- `x**3` term: `-3.43809*x**3`
- `x` terms: `-3.43809*x - 3.43809*x` = `-6.87619*x`
- Cross term: `-0.06600*x*Abs(v)**(1/3)`

So GT = **-1.8997*v - 3.4381*x³ - 6.8762*x - 0.0660*x*|v|^(1/3)**

Key basis functions in GT:
1. `v` (linear in v)
2. `x³`
3. `x` (linear in x)
4. `x*|v|^(1/3)` (cross term with fractional power of |v|)

Note: There is NO `x²` term, NO constant term, NO `t` dependence, NO `x⁵` term, NO `v*x²` term.

The critical unique feature is the `x*|v|^(1/3)` term. This is a very specific nonlinear cross-term that cannot be represented by standard polynomial terms in x and v.

Now let me check each candidate:

**For a candidate to match, it must be able to produce exactly these four basis functions and no others (or set extra terms to zero).**

The problematic term is `x*|v|^(1/3)`. None of the candidates contain `|v|^(1/3)` or any fractional power of v. Let me verify this for each candidate.

Going through all 50 candidates, I need to check if any can produce the `x*|v|^(1/3)` term:

- Most candidates use polynomial terms in v (v, v², v³), polynomial terms in x, cross terms like `v*x²`, `v*x`, exponentials, trigonometric functions, `|v|`, `v*|v|`, `|x|`, `x*|x|`, etc.
- None contain `|v|^(1/3)` or any fractional power of |v|.

The term `x*|v|^(1/3)` is linearly independent from all standard polynomial, exponential, and trigonometric basis functions. It cannot be represented by any combination of:
- `v`, `v²`, `v³`, `v*x²`, `v*x`, `v*|v|`, `|v|`, `x*|x|`, `exp(...)`, `cos(...)`, `sin(...)`, etc.

Since `|v|^(1/3)` is not equivalent to any integer power of v or any other standard function, and this term has a non-zero coefficient (~0.066), no candidate can exactly match the GT.

Let me verify there isn't a candidate with `v**c` or similar flexible power terms... Candidate 32 has `c7*v**c8*x**2` which gives `v^(c8)*x²`, but we need `v^(1/3)*x`, not `v^(c)*x²`. The x-power doesn't match.

After careful review of all 50 candidates, none contain the basis function `x*|v|^(1/3)` and none can produce it through any combination of their terms.
